# New Quizzes - view multi session information | Instructure Developer Documentation Portal

circle-exclamation

**Welcome to Our New API Docs!** This is the new home for all things API (previously at [Canvas LMS REST API Documentationarrow-up-right](https://api.instructure.com/)
).

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_new_quizzes_multiple_session_detection#new-quizzes-view-multi-session-information)

New Quizzes - view multi session information


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_new_quizzes_multiple_session_detection#what-it-does)

What it Does

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_new_quizzes_multiple_session_detection#new-quizzes)

New Quizzes

This permission allows users to view multi-session activity information on the activity log and the moderate page.

### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_new_quizzes_multiple_session_detection#additional-considerations)

Additional Considerations

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_new_quizzes_multiple_session_detection#quiz-settings)

Quiz settings

Educators can enable the Detect Multiple Sessions setting on their quizzes to collect multi-session information on student submissions. This permission determines who can view this data in the activity log and moderate page.

Grades - view all grades


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_view_all_grades#what-it-does)

What it Does

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_view_all_grades#admin-tools-logging-tab)

Admin Tools (Logging tab)

Allows user to search by assignment ID in grade change logs.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_view_all_grades#analytics)

Analytics

Allows user to view student-specific data in Analytics.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_view_all_grades#assignments-speedgrader)

Assignments, SpeedGrader

Allows user to view a link to SpeedGrader from assignments.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_view_all_grades#gradebook)

Gradebook

Allows user to export the Gradebook to a comma separated values (CSV) file.

Allows user to access the Learning Mastery Gradebook (if enabled).

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_view_all_grades#grades)

Grades

Allows user to view student Grades pages.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_view_all_grades#modules)

Modules

Allows user to access the Student Progress page.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_view_all_grades#people-course)

People (Course)

Allows user to view analytics link in the user settings menu.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_view_all_grades#quizzes)

Quizzes

Allows user to view student results, view quiz statistics, and access a quiz in SpeedGrader.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_view_all_grades#rubrics-speedgrader)

Rubrics, SpeedGrader

Allows user to view grader comments on a rubric in SpeedGrader.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_view_all_grades#student-context-card)

Student Context Card

Adds analytics to a student’s context card.

### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_view_all_grades#additional-considerations)

Additional Considerations

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_view_all_grades#admin-tools-grade-change-logs)

Admin Tools (Grade Change Logs)

To search grade change logs, Grades - view change logs must also be enabled.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_view_all_grades#analytics-1)

Analytics

To view student analytics, Analytics - view must also be enabled.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_view_all_grades#gradebook-1)

Gradebook

To view the Gradebook, Course Content - view must also be enabled.

If both Grades - edit and Grades - view all grades are disabled, Gradebook will be hidden from Course Navigation.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_view_all_grades#grades-1)

Grades

To post or hide grades, Grades - edit must also be enabled.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_view_all_grades#modules-1)

Modules

To view module progression, Grades - view all grades must also be enabled.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_view_all_grades#reports)

Reports

To access the Student Interactions report, Reports - manage must also be enabled.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_view_all_grades#student-context-card-1)

Student Context Card

Student Context Cards must be enabled for an account by an admin.

# Manage Groups | Instructure Developer Documentation Portal

circle-exclamation

**Welcome to Our New API Docs!** This is the new home for all things API (previously at [Canvas LMS REST API Documentationarrow-up-right](https://api.instructure.com/)
).

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_groups#manage-groups)

Manage Groups


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_groups#what-it-does)

What it Does

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_groups#groups-add)

Groups - add

Allows user to create account or course groups.

Allows user to add group members to account or course groups.

Allows user to add a group for a group assignment in a course.

Allows user to create course groups created by students.

Allows users to import groups in a course.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_groups#groups-delete)

Groups - delete

Allows user to delete account or course groups.

Allows user to remove students from account or course groups.

Allows user to move group members to another group in an account or course.

Allows user to assign a student group leader in an account or course.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_groups#groups-manage)

Groups - manage

Allows user to edit account and course groups.

Allows user to view the Clone Group Set button for an account or course group.

Allows user to randomly assign users to an account or course group.

Allows user to add users to an account or course group.

Allows user to move group members to another group in an account or course.

Allows user to assign a student group leader in an account or course.

### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_groups#additional-considerations)

Additional Considerations

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_groups#groups-add-1)

Groups - add

To add account level groups via CSV, SIS Data - import must also be enabled.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_groups#groups)

Groups

If this permission is disabled, at the account level, the user cannot view any existing account groups. At the course level, the user can view, but not access, any existing groups, including groups created by students.

To view account-level groups, Users - view list must also be enabled.

To view all student groups in a course, Groups - view all student groups must also be enabled.

By default, students can always create groups in a course. To restrict students from creating groups, Courses - manage must be enabled, and the Let students organize their own groups checkbox in Course Settings must not be selected.

To access the People page and view course groups, Users - view list must also be enabled.

* * *

This documentation is generated directly from the Canvas LMS source code, available [on Githubarrow-up-right](https://github.com/instructure/canvas-lms)
.

[PreviousManage Differentiation Tagschevron-left](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_differentiation_tags)
[NextManage LTIchevron-right](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_lti)

Last updated 6 months ago

Was this helpful?

*   [Manage Groups](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_groups#manage-groups)
    
*   [What it Does](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_groups#what-it-does)
    
*   [Additional Considerations](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_groups#additional-considerations)

# Statistics - view | Instructure Developer Documentation Portal

circle-exclamation

).

Statistics - view


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_view_statistics#what-it-does)

What it Does

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_view_statistics#account-statistics)

Account Statistics

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_view_statistics#admin-tools-logging-tab)

Admin Tools (Logging tab)

Allows user to generate login/logout activity report in Admin Tools.

### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_view_statistics#additional-considerations)

Additional Considerations

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_view_statistics#admin-tools-logging-tab-1)

Admin Tools (Logging tab)

If Statistics - view or Users - manage login details is enabled, the user will be able to generate login/logout activity in Admin Tools. To hide the login/logout activity option in Admin Tools, both of these permissions need to be disabled.

People (Account)

To view user page views, Users - view list must also be enabled.

Subaccounts

Not available at the subaccount level.

# Users - Temporary Enrollments | Instructure Developer Documentation Portal

circle-exclamation

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_temporary_enrollments#users-temporary-enrollments)

Users - Temporary Enrollments


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_temporary_enrollments#what-it-does)

What it Does

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_temporary_enrollments#manage-temporary-enrollments)

Manage Temporary Enrollments

Temporarily enroll a user into a course. This temporary enrollment is paired up with another enrollment within the course.

The temporarily enrolled user can only view and participate in a course between the start and end dates that were chosen when making the temporary enrollment.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_temporary_enrollments#temporary-enrollments-add)

Temporary Enrollments - add

Allows users to add a temporary enrollment with a start date, end date, and role

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_temporary_enrollments#temporary-enrollments-edit)

Temporary Enrollments - edit

Allows users to edit an existing temporary enrollment

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_temporary_enrollments#temporary-enrollments-delete)

Temporary Enrollments - delete

Allows users to delete a temporary enrollment

* * *

.

# Users - Observers | Instructure Developer Documentation Portal

circle-exclamation

**Welcome to Our New API Docs!** This is the new home for all things API (previously at [Canvas LMS REST API Documentationarrow-up-right](https://api.instructure.com/)
).

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_course_observer_enrollments#users-observers)

Users - Observers


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_course_observer_enrollments#what-it-does)

What it Does

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_course_observer_enrollments#observers-add)

Observers - add

Allows user to add observers to a course from the account Courses page.

Allows user to add observers to a course.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_course_observer_enrollments#observers-remove)

Observers - remove

Allows user to remove observers from a course.

Allows user to deactivate observers in a course.

### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_course_observer_enrollments#additional-considerations)

Additional Considerations

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_course_observer_enrollments#courses-account)

Courses (Account)

If the Open Registration account setting is enabled, users with this permission can add observers to a course from the Courses page via email address or login ID even if an observer does not already have a Canvas account.

To add a user via SIS ID, SIS Data - manage must also be enabled.

To access the account Courses page, Courses - view list must be enabled.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_course_observer_enrollments#people-course)

People (Course)

If an enrollment is created via SIS, only admins can remove the enrollment from a course.

To remove a user via SIS ID, SIS Data - manage must also be enabled.

* * *

This documentation is generated directly from the Canvas LMS source code, available [on Githubarrow-up-right](https://github.com/instructure/canvas-lms)
.

# Grades - view change logs | Instructure Developer Documentation Portal

circle-exclamation

**Welcome to Our New API Docs!** This is the new home for all things API (previously at [Canvas LMS REST API Documentationarrow-up-right](https://api.instructure.com/)
).

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_view_grade_changes#grades-view-change-logs)

Grades - view change logs


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_view_grade_changes#what-it-does)

What it Does

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_view_grade_changes#admin-tools-logging-tab)

Admin Tools (Logging tab)

Determines visibility of the Grade Change Activity option in the Admin Tools Logging tab.

### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_view_grade_changes#additional-considerations)

Additional Considerations

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_view_grade_changes#admin-tools-logging-tab-1)

Admin Tools (Logging tab)

To search by grader or student ID, Users - view must also be enabled.

To search by course ID or assignment ID, Grades - edit must also be enabled.

To search by assignment ID only, Grades - view all grades must also be enabled.

# SIS Data - read | Instructure Developer Documentation Portal

circle-exclamation

**Welcome to Our New API Docs!** This is the new home for all things API (previously at [Canvas LMS REST API Documentationarrow-up-right](https://api.instructure.com/)
).

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_read_sis#sis-data-read)

SIS Data - read


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_read_sis#what-it-does)

What it Does

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_read_sis#course-settings)

Course Settings

Allows user to view a course’s SIS ID.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_read_sis#people-account)

People (Account)

Allows user to view the SIS ID in a user’s login details.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_read_sis#people-course)

People (Course)

Allows user to view user SIS IDs in a course People page.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_read_sis#quizzes)

Quizzes

Allows user to view the user SIS ID column in the Quiz Item Analysis CSV file.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_read_sis#sis)

SIS

Governs account-related SIS IDs (i.e., subaccount SIS ID).

### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_read_sis#additional-considerations)

Additional Considerations

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_read_sis#account-and-subaccount)

Account and Subaccount

Users and terms are located at the account, so the SIS endpoint always confirms the user’s permissions according to account.

Subaccounts only have ownership of courses and sections; they do not own user data. Subaccount admins are not able to view SIS information unless they are also granted an instructor role in a course.

Subaccount admins are not able to view SIS information unless they are also granted an instructor role in a course.

Subaccount admins cannot view SIS information without the course association, as the instructor role has permission to read SIS data at the account level.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_read_sis#people-account-1)

People (Account)

To view a user’s login details, Users - view list and Modify login details for users must also both be enabled.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_read_sis#people-course-1)

People (Course)

To add or remove users to a course, the appropriate Users permission must be enabled (e.g. Users - Teachers).

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_read_sis#sis-import)

SIS Import

To manage SIS data, SIS Data - manage must be enabled.

If SIS Data - manage is enabled and SIS Data - read is disabled, the account permission overrides the course permission.

If SIS Data - manage is disabled and SIS Data - read is enabled, users can only view course, user, and subaccount SIS IDs.

To disallow users from viewing any SIS IDs at the course level, SIS Data - manage and SIS Data - read must both be disabled.

* * *

This documentation is generated directly from the Canvas LMS source code, available [on Githubarrow-up-right](https://github.com/instructure/canvas-lms)
.

[PreviousSIS Data - managechevron-left](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_sis)
[NextSite Admin - Rate Limitingchevron-right](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_rate_limiting)

Last updated 6 months ago

Was this helpful?

*   [SIS Data - read](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_read_sis#sis-data-read)
    
*   [What it Does](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_read_sis#what-it-does)
    
*   [Additional Considerations](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_read_sis#additional-considerations)

Manage Course Files


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

###

What it Does

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_files#course-files-add)

Course Files - add

Allows user to import a zip file.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_files#course-files-edit)

# Users - Designers | Instructure Developer Documentation Portal

circle-exclamation

**Welcome to Our New API Docs!** This is the new home for all things API (previously at [Canvas LMS REST API Documentationarrow-up-right](https://api.instructure.com/)
).

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_course_designer_enrollments#users-designers)

Users - Designers


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_course_designer_enrollments#what-it-does)

What it Does

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_course_designer_enrollments#designers-add)

Designers - add

Allows user to add designers to a course from the account Courses page.

Allows user to add designers to a course.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_course_designer_enrollments#designers-remove)

Designers - remove

Allows user to remove designers from a course.

Allows user to deactivate designers in a course.

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_course_designer_enrollments#additional-considerations)

Additional Considerations

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_course_designer_enrollments#courses-account)

Courses (Account)

If the Open Registration account setting is enabled, users with this permission can add designers to a course from the Courses page via email address or login ID even if a designer does not already have a Canvas account.

To add a user via SIS ID, SIS Data - manage must also be enabled.

To access the account Courses page, Courses - view list must be enabled.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_course_designer_enrollments#people-course)

People (Course)

If an enrollment is created via SIS, only admins can remove the enrollment from a course.

To remove a user via SIS ID, SIS Data - manage must also be enabled.

# Users - generate observer pairing codes for students | Instructure Developer Documentation Portal

circle-exclamation

**Welcome to Our New API Docs!** This is the new home for all things API (previously at [Canvas LMS REST API Documentationarrow-up-right](https://api.instructure.com/)
).

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_generate_observer_pairing_code#users-generate-observer-pairing-codes-for-students)

Users - generate observer pairing codes for students


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_generate_observer_pairing_code#what-it-does)

What it Does

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_generate_observer_pairing_code#people-course)

People (Course)

Allows user to generate a pairing code on behalf of a student to share with an observer.

### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_generate_observer_pairing_code#additional-considerations)

Additional Considerations

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_generate_observer_pairing_code#people-course-1)

People (Course)

To generate a pairing code from a student\`s User Settings page, the User - act as permission must also be enabled.

To generate a pairing code from a student\`s User Details page, the Users - allow administrative actions in courses permission must also be enabled.

Pairing codes are only supported when self registration is enabled for the account.

QR codes are not the same as pairing codes and are only used to help users log into their own accounts via the Canvas mobile apps. To disable QR code logins for all users in your account, please contact your Customer Success Manager.

* * *

This documentation is generated directly from the Canvas LMS source code, available [on Githubarrow-up-right](https://github.com/instructure/canvas-lms)
.

# Manage Assignments and Quizzes | Instructure Developer Documentation Portal

circle-exclamation

**Welcome to Our New API Docs!** This is the new home for all things API (previously at [Canvas LMS REST API Documentationarrow-up-right](https://api.instructure.com/)
).

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_assignments_and_quizzes#manage-assignments-and-quizzes)

Manage Assignments and Quizzes


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_assignments_and_quizzes#what-it-does)

What it Does

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_assignments_and_quizzes#assignments-and-quizzes-add)

Assignments and Quizzes - add

Allows user to add assignments in a course.

Allows user to add assignment groups in a course.

Allows user to duplicate assignments in a course.

Allows user to add new assignments to a module.

Allows user to add new question banks to a course or account.

Allows user to add new questions to new or existing question banks in a course or account.

Allows user to add quizzes in a course.

Allows user to duplicate quizzes in a course.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_assignments_and_quizzes#assignments-and-quizzes-edit)

Assignments and Quizzes - edit

Allows user to edit and publish/unpublish assignments.

Allows user to manage assignment settings.

Allows user to weight assignment groups.

Allows user to edit lock settings on the Assignments and Quizzes index pages.

Allows user to share an assignment to Commons.

Allows user to share a quiz to Commons.

Determines visibility and management of the Question Banks link in Account Navigation.

Allows user to edit and publish/unpublish quizzes.

Allows user to edit question banks in a course or account.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_assignments_and_quizzes#assignments-and-quizzes-delete)

Assignments and Quizzes - delete

Allows user to delete assignments in a course.

Allows user to delete assignment groups in a course.

Allows user to delete quizzes in a course.

Allows user to delete question banks in a course or account.

### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_assignments_and_quizzes#additional-considerations)

Additional Considerations

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_assignments_and_quizzes#assignments)

Assignments

To access the Assignments Index Page, Course Content - view must be enabled.

To differentiate assignments to individual students, Users - view list must also be enabled.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_assignments_and_quizzes#blueprint-courses)

Blueprint Courses

To edit lock settings from the Assignments index page, Blueprint Courses - add / edit / associate / delete and Courses - manage must also be enabled.

If Blueprint Courses - add / edit / associate / delete and Courses - manage are enabled, but Assignments and Quizzes - edit is not enabled, blueprint lock settings for an assignment can be managed from the assignment’s details page.

To edit lock settings on an individual quiz, or on the Quizzes index page, Blueprint Courses - add / edit / associate / delete and Courses - manage must also be enabled.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_assignments_and_quizzes#course-settings)

Course Settings

To import assignments and quizzes using the Course Import Tool, Course Content - add / edit / delete must be enabled.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_assignments_and_quizzes#discussions)

Discussions

These permissions do not manage Discussions. Discussions are managed via individual Discussion permissions.

To edit assignment details on individual discussions, Discussions - manage must also be enabled.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_assignments_and_quizzes#grades)

Grades

To manage moderated grading, Grades - Select final grade for moderation must also be enabled.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_assignments_and_quizzes#quizzes)

Quizzes

To access the Quizzes Index Page, Course Content - view must be enabled.

To moderate a quiz, Grades - edit must also be enabled.

To access item banks for a course or account, Item Banks - manage account must also be enabled.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_assignments_and_quizzes#rubrics)

Rubrics

Disabling the Assignments and Quizzes - add permission will override (if enabled) the Rubrics - add / edit / delete permission, preventing user from creating rubrics for an individual assignment.

Disabling the Assignments and Quizzes - edit permission will override (if enabled) the Rubrics - add / edit / delete permission, preventing users from editing rubrics from an individual assignment.

Disabling the Assignments and Quizzes - delete permission will override (if enabled) the Rubrics - add / edit / delete permission, preventing user from deleting rubrics for an individual assignment.

* * *

This documentation is generated directly from the Canvas LMS source code, available [on Githubarrow-up-right](https://github.com/instructure/canvas-lms)
.

[PreviousManage Account Calendarschevron-left](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_account_calendar)
[NextManage Course Contentchevron-right](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_course_content)

Last updated 6 months ago

*   [Manage Assignments and Quizzes](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_assignments_and_quizzes#manage-assignments-and-quizzes)

# Outcome Mastery Scales - add / edit | Instructure Developer Documentation Portal

circle-exclamation

**Welcome to Our New API Docs!** This is the new home for all things API (previously at [Canvas LMS REST API Documentationarrow-up-right](https://api.instructure.com/)
).

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_proficiency_scales#outcome-mastery-scales-add-edit)

Outcome Mastery Scales - add / edit


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_proficiency_scales#what-it-does)

What it Does

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_proficiency_scales#outcomes)

Outcomes

Allows user to view the Outcomes Mastery tab and set outcome mastery scales at the account and course levels.

### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_proficiency_scales#additional-considerations)

Additional Considerations

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_proficiency_scales#feature-option)

Feature Option

This permission requires the Account and Course Level Outcome Mastery Scales feature option, which must be enabled by a Customer Success Manager.

This feature affects existing data for an entire account.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_proficiency_scales#outcomes-1)

Outcomes

If the feature option is enabled, and this permission is enabled, the Outcomes page includes three tabs: Manage, Mastery, and Calculation.

To access the Calculation tab, the Outcome Proficiency Calculations - add / edit permission must also be enabled. To access the Manage tab, the Learning Outcomes - add / edit / delete permission must also be enabled.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_proficiency_scales#rubrics)

Rubrics

If this permission is enabled, the Learning Mastery tab displays on the Outcomes page instead of the Rubrics page.

* * *

This documentation is generated directly from the Canvas LMS source code, available [on Githubarrow-up-right](https://github.com/instructure/canvas-lms)
.

[PreviousNotifications - viewchevron-left](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_view_notifications)
[NextOutcome Proficiency Calculations - add / editchevron-right](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_proficiency_calculations)

Last updated 6 months ago

Was this helpful?

# Site Admin - Rate Limiting | Instructure Developer Documentation Portal

circle-exclamation

**Welcome to Our New API Docs!** This is the new home for all things API (previously at [Canvas LMS REST API Documentationarrow-up-right](https://api.instructure.com/)
).

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_rate_limiting#site-admin-rate-limiting)

Site Admin - Rate Limiting


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_rate_limiting#what-it-does)

What it Does

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_rate_limiting#rate-limiting-add)

Rate Limiting - add

Allows user to create new rate limit settings for external tools and integrations.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_rate_limiting#rate-limiting-edit)

Rate Limiting - edit

Allows user to modify existing rate limit settings, including changing rate limit values and comments.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_rate_limiting#rate-limiting-delete)

Rate Limiting - delete

Allows user to remove rate limit settings for external tools and integrations.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_rate_limiting#rate-limiting-view)

Rate Limiting - view

Allows user to view all rate limit settings and their details.

### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_rate_limiting#additional-considerations)

Additional Considerations

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_rate_limiting#site-admin-only)

Site Admin Only

This permission is only available to Site Admin users and requires the api\_rate\_limits feature flag to be enabled.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_rate_limiting#external-tools)

External Tools

Rate limiting settings apply to external tools and integrations that use OAuth client configurations with throttling parameters.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_rate_limiting#utid-integration)

UTID Integration

This feature supports UTID (Unified Tool ID) based rate limiting for partner tools and products.

* * *

This documentation is generated directly from the Canvas LMS source code, available [on Githubarrow-up-right](https://github.com/instructure/canvas-lms)

circle-exclamation

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

What it Does

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_sections#course-sections-add)

Course Sections - add

Allows user to add course sections in Course Settings.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_sections#course-sections-edit)

Course Sections - edit

Allows user to rename course sections.

Allows user to change start and end dates for course sections.

Allows user to cross-list sections.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_sections#course-sections-delete)

Allows user to delete course sections.

####

Cross-Listing

To cross-list sections, Course Sections - edit and Courses - manage must also be enabled.

# Users - act as | Instructure Developer Documentation Portal

circle-exclamation

**Welcome to Our New API Docs!** This is the new home for all things API (previously at [Canvas LMS REST API Documentationarrow-up-right](https://api.instructure.com/)
).

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_become_user#users-act-as)

Users - act as


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_become_user#what-it-does)

What it Does

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_become_user#people-account)

People (Account)

Allows user to act as other users in the account.

This permission should only be assigned to users that your institution has authorized to act as other users in your entire Canvas account.

Users with this permission may be able to use the Act as feature to manage account settings, view and adjust grades, access user information, etc.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_become_user#student-context-card)

Student Context Card

Allows user to access the Act as User link on student context cards.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_become_user#speedgrader)

SpeedGrader

Allows user to delete a submission file.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_become_user#people-course)

People (Course)

Allows user to view Login IDs in a course People page.

### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_become_user#additional-considerations)

Additional Considerations

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_become_user#api)

API

The Roles API refers to this permission as become\_user.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_become_user#people-account-1)

People (Account)

To view the list of users in an account, Users - view list must be enabled.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_become_user#student-context-card-1)

Student Context Card

Student Context Cards must be enabled for an account by an admin.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_become_user#subaccounts)

Subaccounts

Not available at the subaccount level.

* * *

This documentation is generated directly from the Canvas LMS source code, available [on Githubarrow-up-right](https://github.com/instructure/canvas-lms)
.

[PreviousUsers - Temporary Enrollmentschevron-left](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_temporary_enrollments)
[NextUsers - allow administrative actions in courseschevron-right](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_allow_course_admin_actions)

Last updated 6 months ago

Was this helpful?

*   [Users - act as](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_become_user#users-act-as)

# Users - view login IDs | Instructure Developer Documentation Portal

circle-exclamation

**Welcome to Our New API Docs!** This is the new home for all things API (previously at [Canvas LMS REST API Documentationarrow-up-right](https://api.instructure.com/)
).

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_view_user_logins#users-view-login-ids)

Users - view login IDs


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_view_user_logins#what-it-does)

What it Does

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_view_user_logins#people-account-course)

People (Account, Course)

Allows user to search for other users by Login ID in the account People page.

### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_view_user_logins#additional-considerations)

Additional Considerations

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_view_user_logins#people-account-course-1)

People (Account, Course)

To access the People page, Users - view list must be enabled.

If this permission is enabled, and if Users - view primary email address is disabled, users will see email addresses used as login IDs.

To view login IDs, Users - allow administrative actions in courses must also be enabled.

* * *

This documentation is generated directly from the Canvas LMS source code, available [on Githubarrow-up-right](https://github.com/instructure/canvas-lms)
.

circle-exclamation

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_proxy_assignment_submission#submission-submit-on-behalf-of-student)

Submission - Submit on behalf of student


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_proxy_assignment_submission#what-it-does)

What it Does

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_proxy_assignment_submission#submissions)

Submissions

Allows instructors to submit file attachments on behalf of a student.

### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_proxy_assignment_submission#additional-considerations)

Additional Considerations

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_proxy_assignment_submission#submissions-1)

Submissions

Once enabled, this option is visible in gradebook for instructors.

Instructors are not bound by attempt limits, but an instructor's submission WILL count as a student's attempt.

# Storage Quotas - manage | Instructure Developer Documentation Portal

circle-exclamation

**Welcome to Our New API Docs!** This is the new home for all things API (previously at [Canvas LMS REST API Documentationarrow-up-right](https://api.instructure.com/)
).

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_storage_quotas#storage-quotas-manage)

Storage Quotas - manage


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_storage_quotas#what-it-does)

What it Does

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_storage_quotas#quotas-account-settings)

Quotas (Account Settings)

Allows user to view and manage Quotas tab in Account Settings. User can set default course, user, and group storage quotes.

# Web Conferences - create | Instructure Developer Documentation Portal

circle-exclamation

**Welcome to Our New API Docs!** This is the new home for all things API (previously at [Canvas LMS REST API Documentationarrow-up-right](https://api.instructure.com/)
).

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_create_conferences#web-conferences-create)

Web Conferences - create


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_create_conferences#what-it-does)

What it Does

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_create_conferences#conferences)

Conferences

Allows user to create new conferences in courses and groups.

Allows user to start conferences they created.

### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_create_conferences#additional-considerations)

Additional Considerations

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_create_conferences#conferences-1)

Conferences

To allow full management of conferences created by the user or others, the Course Content permission must also be enabled.

To end a long-running conference, the Course Content permission must be enabled.

If the Course Content permission enabled and Web Conferences - create is disabled, the user can still manage conferences.

# Manage Course Content | Instructure Developer Documentation Portal

circle-exclamation

**Welcome to Our New API Docs!** This is the new home for all things API (previously at [Canvas LMS REST API Documentationarrow-up-right](https://api.instructure.com/)
).

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_course_content#manage-course-content)

Manage Course Content


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_course_content#what-it-does)

What it Does

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_course_content#course-content-add)

Course Content - add

Allows user to share course items directly with other users.

Allows user to copy individual course items to another course.

Allows user to view course copy status.

Allows user to create content migrations.

Allows user to create blackout dates.

Allows user to add events to Calendar List View Dashboard via the Add to Student To-Do checkbox.

Allows user to create a course pace via Course Pacing.

Allows user to import resources from Commons into a course.

Allows user to import content using the Course Import Tool.

Allows user to add non-graded discussions to List View Dashboard via the Add to Student To-Do checkbox.

Allows user to create, add items, and duplicate modules.

Allows user to add pages to List View Dashboard via the Add to Student To-Do checkbox.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_course_content#course-content-edit)

Course Content - edit

Allows user to lock / unlock selected announcements individually or in bulk.

Allows user to edit a list of assignment blackout dates.

Allows user to share assignments to Commons or edit previously shared content.

Allows user to edit to-do date on a course Page that supports it.

Allows user to edit Conferences.

Allows user to edit title, and description on all collaborations.

Allows user to update modules (edit module settings, publish, unpublish, batch edit, assign modules).

Allows user to edit content migrations.

Allows user to edit and publish a course pace via Course Pacing.

Allows user to edit the course syllabus.

Allows user to edit course tabs.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_course_content#course-content-delete)

Course Content - delete

Allows user to remove selected announcements individually or in bulk.

Allows user to remove assignment blackout dates.

Allows user to remove collaborators on all collaborations.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_course_content#course-content-add-edit-or-delete)

Course Content - add / edit / or delete

Allows user to have full section visibility when viewing announcements.

Allows user to access the Attendance tool.

Allows user to view Course Status, Choose Home Page, and Course Setup Checklist buttons in the Home page.

Allows user to access the Chat tool.

Allows user to view course Conferences.

Allows user to view and list content migrations.

Allows user to view a content migration content list by type.

Allows user access to LTI sub navigation tool selection for assignment syllabus configuration.

Allows user to view or retrieve a list of assignment blackout dates.

Allows user to view a content migration notice to an "import in progress".

Allows user to view previously created collaborations.

Allows user to view and list course paces via Course Pacing.

Allows user to view and initiate course link validation.

### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_course_content#additional-considerations)

Additional Considerations

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_course_content#attendance)

Attendance

The Attendance tool must be enabled by your Canvas admin.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_course_content#chat)

Chat

The Chat tool must be enabled by your Canvas admin.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_course_content#commons)

Commons

To share a Discussion to Commons, Discussions - view must also be enabled.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_course_content#course-home-page)

Course Home Page

Teachers, designers, and TAs can select a course home page without the Course content - add / edit / delete permission.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_course_content#course-settings)

Course Settings

The Course Status buttons (unpublished and published) are only displayed until a student submission is received. Courses cannot be unpublished with student submissions.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_course_content#modules)

Modules

Module items cannot be unpublished if there are student submissions.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_course_content#course-pacing)

Course Pacing

Course Pacing feature preview must be enabled in your institution.

* * *

This documentation is generated directly from the Canvas LMS source code, available [on Githubarrow-up-right](https://github.com/instructure/canvas-lms)
.

[PreviousManage Assignments and Quizzeschevron-left](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_assignments_and_quizzes)
[NextManage Course Fileschevron-right](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_files)

Last updated 6 months ago

Was this helpful?

*   [Manage Course Content](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_course_content#manage-course-content)
    
*   [What it Does](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_course_content#what-it-does)
    
*   [Additional Considerations](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_course_content#additional-considerations)

# Manage Pages | Instructure Developer Documentation Portal

circle-exclamation

**Welcome to Our New API Docs!** This is the new home for all things API (previously at [Canvas LMS REST API Documentationarrow-up-right](https://api.instructure.com/)
).

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_wiki#manage-pages)

Manage Pages


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_wiki#what-it-does)

What it Does

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_wiki#pages-create)

Pages - create

Allows user to create course pages.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_wiki#pages-delete)

Pages - delete

Allows user to delete course pages.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_wiki#pages-update)

Pages - update

Allows user to edit course pages.

Allows user to define users allowed to edit the page.

Allows user to add page to student to-do list.

Allows user to publish and unpublish pages.

Allows user to view page history and set front page.

Allows user to edit Blueprint Course lock settings in the Pages index page and for an individual page in a Blueprint master course.

### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_wiki#additional-considerations)

Additional Considerations

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_wiki#blueprint-courses)

Blueprint Courses

Blueprint courses must be enabled for an account by an admin.

To edit lock settings on the Pages index page, Pages - update, Blueprint Courses - add / edit / associate / delete, and Courses - manage.

However, if these additional permissions are enabled, but the Pages - update permission is not enabled, the user can still adjust content lock settings on individual pages in a Blueprint Master Course.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_wiki#student-page-history)

Student Page History

Students can edit and view page history if allowed in the options for an individual page.

* * *

This documentation is generated directly from the Canvas LMS source code, available [on Githubarrow-up-right](https://github.com/instructure/canvas-lms)
.

# Users - manage login details | Instructure Developer Documentation Portal

circle-exclamation

**Welcome to Our New API Docs!** This is the new home for all things API (previously at [Canvas LMS REST API Documentationarrow-up-right](https://api.instructure.com/)
).

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_user_logins#users-manage-login-details)

Users - manage login details


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_user_logins#what-it-does)

What it Does

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_user_logins#people-account)

People (Account)

Allows user to create accounts for new users.

Allows user to remove and merge users in an account.

Allows user to modify user account details.

Allows user to view and modify login information for a user.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_user_logins#admin-tools-logging-tab)

Admin Tools (Logging tab)

Allows user to generate login/logout activity report in Admin Tools.

### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_user_logins#additional-considerations)

Additional Considerations

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_user_logins#admin-tools-logging-tab-1)

Admin Tools (Logging tab)

If Users - manage login details or Statistics - view is enabled, the user will be able to generate login/logout activity in Admin Tools. To hide the login/logout activity option in Admin Tools, both of these permissions need to be disabled.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_user_logins#people-account-1)

People (Account)

To view users and user account details, Users - view list must be enabled.

To change user passwords, Users - view must also be enabled.

To view a user’s SIS ID, SIS Data - manage or SIS Data - read must also be enabled.

To view a user’s Integration ID, SIS Data - manage must also be enabled.

To merge users, the Self Service User Merge feature option must also be enabled.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_user_logins#people-course)

People (Course)

To add or remove users to a course, the appropriate Users permission must be enabled (e.g. Users - Teachers).

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_user_logins#subaccounts)

Subaccounts

Not available at the subaccount level.

* * *

This documentation is generated directly from the Canvas LMS source code, available [on Githubarrow-up-right](https://github.com/instructure/canvas-lms)
.

[PreviousUsers - generate observer pairing codes for studentschevron-left](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_generate_observer_pairing_code)
[NextUsers - manage observerschevron-right](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_user_observers)

Last updated 6 months ago

Was this helpful?

# Users - Students | Instructure Developer Documentation Portal

circle-exclamation

**Welcome to Our New API Docs!** This is the new home for all things API (previously at [Canvas LMS REST API Documentationarrow-up-right](https://api.instructure.com/)
).

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_course_student_enrollments#users-students)

Users - Students


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_course_student_enrollments#what-it-does)

What it Does

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_course_student_enrollments#students-add)

Students - add

Allows user to add students to a course from the account Courses page.

Allows user to update a student’s section enrollment or role.

Allows user to add students to a course.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_course_student_enrollments#students-remove)

Students - remove

Allows user to remove students from a course.

Allows user to remove a student’s section enrollment or role.

Allows user to deactivate students in a course.

### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_course_student_enrollments#additional-considerations)

Additional Considerations

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_course_student_enrollments#courses-account)

Courses (Account)

If the Open Registration account setting is enabled, users with this permission can add students to a course from the Courses page via email address or login ID even if a student does not already have a Canvas account.

To add a user via SIS ID, SIS Data - manage must also be enabled.

To access the account Courses page, Courses - view list must be enabled.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_course_student_enrollments#people-course)

People (Course)

If an enrollment is created via SIS, only admins can remove the enrollment from a course.

To remove a user via SIS ID, SIS Data - manage must also be enabled.

* * *

This documentation is generated directly from the Canvas LMS source code, available [on Githubarrow-up-right](https://github.com/instructure/canvas-lms)
.

[NextUsers - TAschevron-right](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_course_ta_enrollments)

# SIS Data - manage | Instructure Developer Documentation Portal

circle-exclamation

**Welcome to Our New API Docs!** This is the new home for all things API (previously at [Canvas LMS REST API Documentationarrow-up-right](https://api.instructure.com/)
).

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_sis#sis-data-manage)

SIS Data - manage


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_sis#what-it-does)

What it Does

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_sis#account-navigation)

Account Navigation

Determines visibility of SIS Import link in Account Navigation.

Allows user to view the previous SIS import dates, errors, and imported items.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_sis#course-settings)

Course Settings

Allows user to edit the course SIS ID.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_sis#people-account)

People (Account)

Allows user to view and edit the SIS ID and Integration ID in a user’s Login Details.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_sis#people-course)

People (Course)

Allows user to edit the course SIS ID.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_sis#subaccount-settings)

Subaccount Settings

Allows user to view and insert data in the SIS ID field.

### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_sis#additional-considerations)

Additional Considerations

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_sis#course-settings-1)

Course Settings

To edit course settings, Courses - manage must be enabled.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_sis#people-account-1)

People (Account)

To view or edit a user’s SIS ID or Integration ID, Users - view list and Users - manage login details must also both be enabled.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_sis#people-course-1)

People (Course)

If this permission is enabled, users do not need the SIS Data - read permission enabled. The account permission overrides the course permission.

To disallow users from managing SIS IDs at the course level, SIS Data - manage and SIS Data - read must both be disabled.

To add or remove users to a course, the appropriate Users permission must be enabled (e.g. Users - Teachers).

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_sis#sis-import)

SIS Import

To import SIS data, SIS Data - import must also be enabled.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_sis#subaccounts)

Subaccounts

Not available at the subaccount level.

* * *

This documentation is generated directly from the Canvas LMS source code, available [on Githubarrow-up-right](https://github.com/instructure/canvas-lms)
.

[PreviousSIS Data - importchevron-left](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_import_sis)
[NextSIS Data - readchevron-right](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_read_sis)

Last updated 6 months ago

Was this helpful?

*   [SIS Data - manage](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_sis#sis-data-manage)

# Users - manage students in courses | Instructure Developer Documentation Portal

circle-exclamation

**Welcome to Our New API Docs!** This is the new home for all things API (previously at [Canvas LMS REST API Documentationarrow-up-right](https://api.instructure.com/)
).

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_students#users-manage-students-in-courses)

Users - manage students in courses


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_students#what-it-does)

What it Does

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_students#people-course)

People (Course)

Allows user to view login ID information for students.

Allows user to view prior enrollments.

Allows user to access a user’s settings menu and user details.

Allows user to resend course invitations from the Course People page.

### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_students#additional-considerations)

Additional Considerations

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_students#courses-account)

Courses (Account)

To access the account Courses page, Courses - view list must be enabled.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_students#people-course-1)

People (Course)

To add or remove a student to or from a course, the Users - Student permission must be enabled.

To view the list of users in the course, Users - view list must be enabled.

To view SIS IDs, SIS Data - read must be enabled.

To edit a student’s section, Conversations - send to individual course members must also be enabled.

* * *

This documentation is generated directly from the Canvas LMS source code, available [on Githubarrow-up-right](https://github.com/instructure/canvas-lms)
.

Last updated 6 months ago

# Manage LTI | Instructure Developer Documentation Portal

circle-exclamation

**Welcome to Our New API Docs!** This is the new home for all things API (previously at [Canvas LMS REST API Documentationarrow-up-right](https://api.instructure.com/)
).

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_lti#manage-lti)

Manage LTI


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_lti#what-it-does)

What it Does

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_lti#lti-add)

LTI - add

Allows user to manually add an app in Account Settings.

Allows user to add external app icons to the Rich Content Editor toolbar.

Allows user to manually add an app in Course Settings.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_lti#lti-delete)

LTI - delete

Allows user to manually delete an app in Account Settings.

Allows user to manually delete an app in Course Settings.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_lti#lti-edit)

LTI - edit

Allows user to edit configurations for manually added external apps.

### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_lti#additional-considerations)

Additional Considerations

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_lti#external-apps)

External Apps

If LTI - add is disabled, users can still install approved apps through the Canvas App Center (if enabled for your institution). However, if LTI - delete is not enabled, they cannot delete manually added external apps.

* * *

This documentation is generated directly from the Canvas LMS source code, available [on Githubarrow-up-right](https://github.com/instructure/canvas-lms)
.

# Users - Teachers | Instructure Developer Documentation Portal

circle-exclamation

**Welcome to Our New API Docs!** This is the new home for all things API (previously at [Canvas LMS REST API Documentationarrow-up-right](https://api.instructure.com/)
).

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_course_teacher_enrollments#users-teachers)

Users - Teachers


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_course_teacher_enrollments#what-it-does)

What it Does

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_course_teacher_enrollments#teachers-add)

Teachers - add

Allows user to add teachers to a course from the account Courses page.

Allows user to add teachers to a course.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_course_teacher_enrollments#teachers-remove)

Teachers - remove

Allows user to remove teachers from a course.

Allows user to deactivate teachers in a course.

### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_course_teacher_enrollments#additional-considerations)

Additional Considerations

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_course_teacher_enrollments#courses-account)

Courses (Account)

If the Open Registration account setting is enabled, users with this permission can add teachers to a course from the Courses page via email address or login ID even if a teacher does not already have a Canvas account.

To add a user via SIS ID, SIS Data - manage must also be enabled.

To access the account Courses page, Courses - view list must be enabled.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_course_teacher_enrollments#people-course)

People (Course)

If an enrollment is created via SIS, only admins can remove the enrollment from a course.

To remove a user via SIS ID, SIS Data - manage must also be enabled.

* * *

This documentation is generated directly from the Canvas LMS source code, available [on Githubarrow-up-right](https://github.com/instructure/canvas-lms)
.

[PreviousUsers - TAschevron-left](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_course_ta_enrollments)
[NextUsers - Temporary Enrollmentschevron-right](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_manage_temporary_enrollments)
