# Users - view list | Instructure Developer Documentation Portal

circle-exclamation

**Welcome to Our New API Docs!** This is the new home for all things API (previously at [Canvas LMS REST API Documentationarrow-up-right](https://api.instructure.com/)
).

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_read_roster#users-view-list)

Users - view list


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_read_roster#what-it-does)

What it Does

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_read_roster#account-navigation)

Account Navigation

Allows user to access the People link in Account Navigation.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_read_roster#admin-tools-logging-tab)

Admin Tools (Logging tab)

Allows user to view login/logout activity of users in Admin Tools.

Allows user to search grade change logs by grader or student in Admin Tools.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_read_roster#assignments)

Assignments

Allows user to differentiate assignments to individual students.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_read_roster#collaborations)

Collaborations

Allows user to view and add users in a collaboration.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_read_roster#conversations)

Conversations

Allows user to send a message in Conversations without selecting a course.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_read_roster#course-navigation)

Course Navigation

Allows user to view the People link in Course Navigation.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_read_roster#groups-course)

Groups (Course)

Allows user to view groups in a course.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_read_roster#people-account)

People (Account)

Allows user to view list of users in the account.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_read_roster#people-course)

People (Course)

Allows user to view list of users in the course People page.

Allows user to view the Prior Enrollments button in the course People page.

### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_read_roster#additional-considerations)

Additional Considerations

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_read_roster#account-groups)

Account Groups

To view account-level groups, Groups - manage must also be enabled.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_read_roster#admin-tools-logging-tab-1)

Admin Tools (Logging tab)

To generate login/logout activity in Admin Tools, Users - manage login details or Statistics - view must also be enabled.

To generate grade change logs in Admin Tools, Grades - view change logs must also be enabled.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_read_roster#courses)

Courses

To add or remove users to a course, the appropriate Users permission must be enabled (e.g. Users - Teachers).

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_read_roster#groups)

Groups

To add groups, Groups - add must also be enabled.

To delete groups, Groups - delete must also be enabled.

To edit groups, Groups - manage must also be enabled.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_read_roster#people-account-1)

People (Account)

To edit user details, modify login details, or change user passwords, Users - manage login details must also be enabled.

To view user page views, Statistics - view must also be enabled.

To act as other users, Users - act as must also be enabled.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_read_roster#people-course-1)

People (Course)

To edit a user’s section, the appropriate Users permission (e.g. Users - Teachers), Users - allow administrative actions in courses, and Conversations - send to individual course members must also be enabled.

* * *

This documentation is generated directly from the Canvas LMS source code, available [on Githubarrow-up-right](https://github.com/instructure/canvas-lms)
.

[PreviousUsers - moderate contentchevron-left](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_moderate_user_content)
[NextUsers - view login IDschevron-right](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_view_user_logins)

Last updated 1 month ago

Was this helpful?

*   [Users - view list](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_read_roster#users-view-list)
    
*   [What it Does](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_read_roster#what-it-does)
    
*   [Additional Considerations](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_read_roster#additional-considerations)

# SIS Data - import | Instructure Developer Documentation Portal

circle-exclamation

**Welcome to Our New API Docs!** This is the new home for all things API (previously at [Canvas LMS REST API Documentationarrow-up-right](https://api.instructure.com/)
).

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_import_sis#sis-data-import)

SIS Data - import


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_import_sis#what-it-does)

What it Does

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_import_sis#account-navigation)

Account Navigation

Determines visibility and management of SIS Import link in Account Navigation.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_import_sis#sis-import)

SIS Import

Allows user to import SIS data.

### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_import_sis#additional-considerations)

Additional Considerations

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_import_sis#sis-import-1)

SIS Import

To manage SIS data, SIS Data - manage must also be enabled.

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_import_sis#subaccounts)

Subaccounts

Not available at the subaccount level

# Item Banks - share with subaccounts | Instructure Developer Documentation Portal

circle-exclamation

**Welcome to Our New API Docs!** This is the new home for all things API (previously at [Canvas LMS REST API Documentationarrow-up-right](https://api.instructure.com/)
).

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_share_banks_with_subaccounts#item-banks-share-with-subaccounts)

Item Banks - share with subaccounts


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_share_banks_with_subaccounts#what-it-does)

What it Does

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_share_banks_with_subaccounts#item-banks)

Item Banks

Allows a user to manage sharing of item banks with subaccounts.

### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_share_banks_with_subaccounts#additional-considerations)

Additional Considerations

#### 

[hashtag](https://developerdocs.instructure.com/services/canvas/permissions/details/file.permissions_share_banks_with_subaccounts#item-banks-1)

Item Banks

If this permission is disabled, users cannot share item banks to subaccounts. When a user with an admin role is granted this permission, the user can share item banks to subaccounts they administer.

This documentation is generated directly from the Canvas LMS source code, available [on Githubarrow-up-right](https://github.com/instructure/canvas-lms)
.
